Business Review
業務回顧


WHO WE ARE                                                                 關於我們
The Group is an integrated communications services provider in Hong        本集團為香港綜合通訊服務機構，擁有本地其中一個
Kong, commanding one of the largest and most influential television        最龐大及最具有影響力的電視觀眾及通訊服務用戶群
audience and communications service user base in town.                     體。

It owns and operates one of the near-universal wireline                    本集團擁有及經營其中一個覆蓋幾近全港的有線電訊
telecommunications network in Hong Kong to provide media and               網絡，向超過 2 百萬住戶提供媒體及電訊服務。
telecommunications services to over 2 million households.

It is also one of the producers of television and multimedia content for   本集團亦是香港其中一家電視與多媒體節目製作商，
distribution over conventional and new media based in Hong Kong,           製作以新聞及資訊、體育與娛樂為主的優質節目，並
with a particular focus on news and information, sports and                通過傳統及新媒體平台發行。
entertainment.

The Group endeavours to sharpen its services to attain higher customer     本集團致力提升服務質素，從而更有效地滿足客戶需
satisfaction, which in turn drives business and revenue performance.       要，以推動業務表現及收入增長。為此，本集團特別
Specifically, the Group pursues the following:                             採取下列營運策略：

(a)   to acquire, produce and distribute quality content meeting local     (a)   購買、製作及發行優質節目，以迎合本地觀眾口
      tastes and needs;                                                          味及需要；

(b)   to invest in infrastructure, network and delivery platforms to       (b)   投放資源於基建、網絡及傳送平台，以提升服務
      enhance service level and customer convenience;                            水平及為客戶帶來更便捷的服務；

(c)   to unlock the value of our infrastructure as well as programming     (c)   善用本集團的基建及節目資源，發揮其在跨平台
      assets for cross-platform and international distribution; and              及國際發行的開展潛能；及

(d)   to continuously better our processes and procedures to always        (d)   持續優化流程及程序，時刻力求達致最佳的成本
      stay cost-effective.                                                       效益。

             invited to rank the importance of each ESG issue via established          個環境、社會及管治議題的重要性進行排序。
             engagement channels and interviews.

             ranking.

             respective Aspects (as defined in the Listing Rules) and KPIs of          關議題如何與《環境、社會及管治指引》的各範疇

         to all potential business partners. Supplier selections and                            會。挑選供應商及採購決定將根據對若干標準（例

         department, compatibility with/conformance to existing                                 使用，循環再造，廢物重用及替代應用」，以盡

10. Prevention of Child and Forced Labour                              10. 防止童工及強制勞工
    The Employment and Compensation & Benefits Policies are              本集團訂立的《僱傭及薪酬與福利政策》，一概遵
    established to meet or exceed the requirements of the                循甚至或超越《僱傭條例》
                                                                                    （香港法例第57章）及《強
    Employment Ordinance (Chapter 57 of the Laws of Hong Kong)           制性公積金計劃條例》的要求。本集團亦採取以
    and the MPFSO. The Group has adopted the following measures          下措施以防止童工及強制勞工的招聘：
    to prevent recruitment of child and forced labour:

    •     Except for child entertainers and summer interns, the          •   除兒童藝員及暑期實習生以外，本集團嚴
          Group shall hold against hiring any candidate who is               禁僱用任何未滿 18 歲的應徵者；
          under 18 years old;
    •     For child entertainers, the Group renews permission to         •   有關兒童藝員，本集團每年會向勞工處申
          employ child entertainers yearly from the Labour                   請相關的許可證續期；及
          Department; and
    •     For summer interns, strict collection of sworn declaration     •   至於暑假實習生，我們須嚴格地收集宣誓
          forms and school endorsement are required to prevent               聲明及學校認可等表格以防止僱用童工。
          child labour.

    Any occurrence of incident would be timely reported to               發生任何事故將適時向管理層報告，並將採取跟
    management and follow up action will be taken. The Group has         進行動。本集團獲強制性公積金計劃管理局嘉許
    received the “Good MPF Employer 5 Years+”, “e-Contribution           為2020/21年度「積金好僱主5年+」、「電子供款獎」
    Award” and “MPF Support Award” in 2020/21 from The                   及「積金推廣獎」，以表揚本集團全面履行僱主法
    Mandatory Provident Fund Schemes Authority for our full              律責任和提供更佳的員工退休福利。

    of better retirement for employees.

     11. Anti-corruption                                                        11. 反貪污
          The Group prohibits bribery and corruption practices. The Group         本集團嚴禁任何貪污賄賂行為。本集團已制定有
          has established the Employee Handbook and the Company                   關道德標準守則的《員工手冊》及《公司政策》，並
          Policy posted on intranet web link regarding standard code of           於內聯網公佈，其列明防止賄賂、賭博、收受捐
          ethics, which states the prevention of bribery, gambling,               獻及內幕交易，以及匯報懷疑違規及涉及利益衝
          collections and insider dealing, as well as the policy on reporting     突事件的政策。
          potential non-compliance and conflict of interest.

          Under the Group’s Code of Conduct, all staff are required to            根據本集團的《操守準則》，所有員工都必須遵守
          abide by the laws on anti-corruption, such as the Prevention of         有關反貪腐的法例，如《防止賄賂條例》   （香港法
          Bribery Ordinance (Chapter 201 of the Laws of Hong Kong). The           例第 201 章）。於報告期內，本集團致力促進商業
          Group strives to promote business ethics and raise awareness            道德及提高意識。本集團向董事及新僱員提供培
          during the Reporting Period, the Group provided trainings and           訓及定期溝通，作為本集團入職計劃的一部分。
          regular communications to the Directors and the new
          employees as part of their orientation programme of the Group.

          There were no incident of non-compliance with anti-corruption           於報告期內概無發生違反反貪污法律及法規的事
          laws and regulations and no concluded legal cases regarding             件，亦無針對本集團或其僱員貪污行為的已完結
          corruption practices brought against the Group or its employees         法律案件。
          during the Reporting Period.

          the Company to decide further action with consultation from             取進一步行動。以匿名方式設置舉報通道供員工
          the legal advisers of the Group. The whistleblowing channel is          舉報不合規事件，令其毋需擔心遭受報復。禁止
          set up in an anonymous manner for staff to report non-                  對舉報人進行任何形式的報復。員工有責任向公
          compliance without the concern of retaliation. Any form of              司匯報任何涉嫌重大違規的行為。本公司會依據

          The Group takes a centralised approach to the Group’s funding                        本集團對本集團的資金及庫務管理以及優化資金
          and treasury management as well as optimisation of the funding                       成本效率採取集中處理方式。管理層 (i) 維持平衡
          cost-efficiency. The management (i) maintains a balanced debt                        的債務及資本融資結構；(ii) 在協定的風險範圍內
          and capital financing structure; (ii) ensures secure and optimum                     確保盈餘資金投資的安全及最佳回報；(iii) 監督與
          return on the investment of surplus funds within an agreed risk                      庫務有關的金融風險，包括但不限於利率風險、
          profile; (iii) oversees the treasury related financial risks, including              外幣風險、流動資金風險及信貸風險；(iv) 致力多
          but not limited to interest rate risk, currency risk, liquidity risk and             元擴展資金來源，並保持均衡的到期狀況；及 (v)
          credit risk; (iv) strives to diversify source of funding and maintain                維持適當的監管環境，以在金融市場充分流動的
          a balanced maturity profile; and (v) maintains an appropriate                        條件下維持合適的財務回報。
          control environment to protect the financial return under the
          fluidity financial market conditions.

          The Group’s assets and liabilities are mainly denominated in HK$                     本集團的資產及負債主要以港元及美元（「美元」）
          and United States Dollars (“US$”) and it earns its revenue and                       計值，而其所賺取的收入以及產生的成本及開支
          incurs costs and expenses mainly in HK$ and US$. As HK$ is                           則主要以港元及美元計值。由於港元與美元掛
          pegged to US$, the Group does not expect any significant                             鈎，本集團預期不會因美元兌港元或港元兌美元
          foreign currency exposure arising from the fluctuation of the                        匯率的波動產生任何重大外幣風險。
          US$/HK$ or HK$/US$ exchange rates.

        Board Diversity Policy                                             董事會成員多元化政策
        The Board has adopted the Board Diversity Policy. Under            董事會已採納《董事會成員多元化政策》。
        the Board Diversity Policy, the Company recognises and             根據該政策，本公司明白並深信一個成員
        embraces the benefits of having a diverse Board with a             多元化的董事會對達致可持續的均衡發展
        vision for the Company to achieve a sustainable and                裨益良多。
        balanced development.

        The Board Diversity Policy sets out the approach to               《董事會成員多元化政策》載列達致董事會
        achieve diversity on the Board and the NC has developed           成員多元化的方法，而提名委員會已制定
        the measurable objectives to implement this Policy, taking        實施此政策的可衡量目標，並經計及基於
        into account the factors based on the business model of           本公司業務模式的多項因素及不時的特定
        the Company and specific needs from time to time. In              需求。於達致董事會成員多元化時，本公
        achieving the board diversity, a number of factors,               司會考慮多項因素，包括但不限於文化及
        including but not limited to, cultural and educational            教 育 背 景、性 別、種 族、年 齡、技 能、知
        background, gender, ethnicity, age, skills, knowledge,            識、經驗及服務年限以及董事會認為經計
        experience and length of service and any other factors            及本公司業務模式及特定需要後屬相關及
        that the Board may consider relevant and applicable from          不時適用之其他因素。所有董事會委任均
        time to time taking into account the Company’s business           以用人唯才為原則，同時亦充分顧及董事
        model and specific needs, are considered. All the Board           會成員多元化的裨益。
        appointments are made on merits while having due
        regard for the benefits of diversity on the Board.

        The NC will review the Board Diversity Policy annually to          提名委員會將每年檢討《董事會成員多元化
        ensure its effectiveness, and recommend any appropriate            政策》，以確保其有效性，並建議作出任何
        revisions to ensure it remains relevant to the Company’s           適當修訂，以確保有關政策切合本公司需
        needs and reflects the current regulatory requirements             要並反映目前監管需求及良好企業管治常
        and good corporate governance practices.                           規。

    (I) Risk Governance                                                       (I)   風險管治
          The risk management and internal control systems (the                     本集團的風險管理及內部監控系統（「風險
          “RM&IC Systems”) of the Group comprise a well-defined                     管理及內部監控系統」）是一個明確的管治
          governance structure, with areas of responsibility and                    架構，每個業務及運作單位的責任範圍及
          limits of authority of each business and operational unit                 權力限制均有清晰描述，以確保有效地互
          clearly delineated to ensure effective checks and balances.               相制衡。本集團已遵守內部監控政策、程
          Internal control policies, procedures and guidelines have                 序及指引，以保障資產不會在未經授權下
          been compiled to safeguard assets against unauthorised                    被挪用或出售、妥善保存記錄、保證供內
          use or disposition, to maintain of proper records, to assure              部使用或向外公佈的財務資料均屬可靠，
          of the reliability of financial information for internal use or           以及符合有關法例及規例。
          publication and to comply with relevant legislation and
          regulations.

               The Board acknowledges its ultimate responsibility to                   董事會承認其有最終責任監察內部控制系
               oversee internal control systems, to evaluate and                       統並評估及釐定為達成策略目標所願意承
               determine the nature and extent of the risks it is willing to           擔的風險性質及程度，及維持風險管理及
               take in achieving strategic objectives and for maintaining              內部監控系統，並監察系統是否有效。管
               the RM&IC Systems as well as to monitor their                           理層負責系統的設計、實施及監察。審核
               effectiveness. The management is tasked with the design,                委員會獲董事會授權監督系統，並獲獨立
               implementation and monitoring of the systems. The AC                    專業人士支援以執行內部審核功能，以提
               has been delegated by the Board to oversee the systems                  供風險評估及內部監控的監督。
               and is supported by independent professionals to perform
               the internal audit function, which provides assessment on
               risk and internal control oversight.

               The internal audit function monitors compliance with                    內部審核功能監察遵守政策及準則的情況，
               policies and standards and carries out an analysis and                  以及對本集團的風險管理及內部監控系統
               independent appraisal of the adequacy and effectiveness                 是否足夠及有效進行分析及獨立評估。按
               of the RM&IC Systems across the Group. Findings                         審核委員會已審閱的年度審核計劃，就有
               regarding risk management and internal control matters                  關風險管理及內部監控事宜的調查結果會
               are reported to the AC, in line with the annual audit plan              向審核委員會匯報，並向相關業務及運作
               reviewed by the AC, and communicated to the business                    單位傳達。
               or corporate units concerned.

               Notwithstanding the above, the RM&IC Systems are                        儘管如上所述，風險管理及內部監控系統
               designed to manage the risk rather than eliminate the risk              乃旨在管理風險而非消除未能達成業務目
               of failure to achieve business objectives, and can only                 標的風險，而且只能合理而非絕對地保證
               provide reasonable and not absolute assurance against                   不會出現嚴重誤述或損失。

(H) RISK MANAGEMENT AND INTERNAL                                         (H) 風險管理及內部監控（續）
    CONTROLS (Continued)
    (II) Risk Management Processes and Practices                           (II) 風險管理程序及常規
        The management maintains a risk register to identify                 管理層備存一份風險登記冊，用以識別重
        major risks, which are then categorised into business risks,         大風險，繼而將重大風險歸類為業務風險、
        financial risks, compliance risks, operational risks and other       財務風險、合規風險、營運風險及其他風
        risks. The risks identified are evaluated in terms of                險。已識別的風險按個別發生的可能性、
        individual likelihood of occurrence, severity of                     後果的嚴重性、優先次序及是否存在預警
        consequence, priority and the existence of early warning             來作出評估。管理層會根據評估結果作出
        signal. Based on the results of the assessment, the                  適當應對：接受風險、轉移風險、消除風
        management will determine the appropriate risk response:             險、降低風險或分擔風險，並制訂相應的
        acceptance, transfer, elimination, reduction or sharing, and         控制及緩減措施。管理層會持續檢討風險
        formulate corresponding control activities and mitigation            狀況，亦會不斷更新風險登記冊，任何具
        measures. The risk profile will be reviewed and the risk             重大風險性質及程度的變動均會載入登記
        register will be updated on an ongoing basis to                      冊。內部監控如有任何缺失，則會傳達至
        incorporate any change in the nature and extent of                   負責的各方，採取修正行動。
        significant risks. Internal control deficiencies, if any, are
        communicated to the responsible parties for taking
        corrective action.

        The AC, through independent professionals to perform the             審核委員會透過獨立專業人士按循環方式
        internal audit function, conducts annual review of the               執行內部審核功能，並對風險管理及內部
        effectiveness of the RM&IC Systems and procedures, on a              監控系統及程序的成效每年作出檢討，檢
        rotation of different cycles basis, covering all controls,           討會以上述風險識別及評估方式進行，範
        including financial, operational and compliance controls, by         疇涵蓋所有方面的監控，包括財務監控、
        way of the above risk identification and assessment exercise.        運作監控及合規監控。委員會向業務及企
        Confirmations from the management, in the form of                    業單位主管取得管理層以核證方式確認風
        certification that the risk management and internal control          險管理及內部監控程序行之有效，符合財
        procedures are functioning effectively to meet the                   務匯報、營運及合規需要。
        respective financial reporting, operational and compliance
        needs, is obtained from business and corporate unit heads.

        To ensure timely, fair, accurate and complete disclosure of          為確保適時、公平、準確及完整披露內幕
        inside information and compliance with the applicable laws           消息及符合適用法律及規例，本集團的內
        and regulations, the Group has in place, as an internal              部監控設有《內幕消息披露政策》，為匯報
        control element, a disclosure policy of inside information           及發放內幕消息和保密提供指引。在該政
        providing guidance on reporting and dissemination of                 策下，董事或業務單位主管如發現有任何
        inside information and preservation of confidentiality. Under        潛在╱疑似內幕消息事件，須在實際可行
        the policy, Directors or heads of business units shall report        情況下盡快向主席╱財務總裁匯報，以釐
        to the Chairman/the Chief Financial Officer for any                  定事態發展的性質，及在有需要時作出披
        potential/suspected inside information event as soon as              露。所有員工亦須遵守《操守標準守則》，
        practicable when it materialises for determining the nature          將非公開資料保密。
        of developments, and if required, making disclosure. All staff
        are also required to observe the code of ethical standards to
        keep non-public information confidential.

(M) DIVIDEND POLICY                                                       (M) 股息政策
    The Board has adopted a Dividend Policy (the “Dividend Policy”).        董事會已採納股息政策（「股息政策」）。根據股息
    Under the Dividend Policy, the Board may from time to time pay          政策，董事會可不時向股東派付由董事會酌情宣
    to the Shareholders annual dividends, if any, on the outstanding        派且須於股東大會上批准的已發行普通股的年度
    ordinary Shares declared by and subject to the discretion of the        股息（如有）。此外，董事會可不時於其認為屬適
    Board and must be approved at a general meeting of the                  當時向股東派付中期股息，根據細則及《公司條
    Shareholders. In addition, the Board may from time to time pay          例》的規定，年度股息及中期股息均不得超過董
    to the Shareholders such interim dividends as appear to the             事會建議的金額。
    Board to be justified, both annual dividends and interim
    dividends shall not exceed the amount recommended by the
    Board, in accordance with the provision of the Articles and the
    CO.

    The Board may only consider to make a distribution if the               倘本公司資產淨值的金額不少於其已催繳股本及
    amount of the Company’s net assets is not less than the                 不可分派儲備的總額；及作出該項分派，不會使
    aggregate of the Company’s called up share capital and                  該等資產的款額減至少於本公司已催繳股本及不
    undistributable reserves; and to the extent that, the distribution      可分派儲備的總額，而該項分派亦以此為限，則
    does not reduce the amount of those assets to an amount less            董事會方會考慮作出有關分派。
    than the aggregate of the Company’s called up share capital and
    undistributable reserves.

consolidated financial statements in this annual report.

      SHARE OPTION SCHEME                                                      購股權計劃
      The Company adopted the Share Option Scheme on 24 May 2018               本公司於二零一八年五月二十四日採納購股權計劃，
      which shall be valid and effective for a period of ten years from the    該計劃將自採納日期起十年有效及生效。
      date of adoption.

      Purpose of the scheme:                           The purpose of the Share Option Scheme is to attract and retain the best available
                                                       personnel, to provide additional incentives to the eligible persons, to recognise and
                                                       acknowledge the contributions that the eligible persons have made or may make to
                                                       the Group and to promote the success of the business of the Group.
      計劃的目的：                                           購股權計劃旨在吸引及挽留最佳現有人員、提供額外獎勵予合資格人士、表
                                                       揚及嘉許合資格人士曾經或可能對本集團作出之貢獻並促進本集團之業務成
                                                       就。

      Participants of the scheme:                      Any person who is (or will be on the date of grant) an employee of the Group, a
                                                       Director, a consultant or an advisor, as may be determined by the Directors from
                                                       time to time.
      計劃的參與者：                                          董事可能不時釐定現時（或將於授出日期）身為本集團員工、董事、顧問或諮
                                                       詢人的任何人士。

      Total number of Shares available for issue       As disclosed in the Composite Document and the Joint Announcement, pursuant to
      under the scheme and percentage of issued        the terms of the Share Option Scheme, all outstanding Share Options as at 3 March
      Shares as at the date of this annual report:     2022 automatically lapsed on 3 March 2022. Accordingly, there was no outstanding
                                                       Share Option as at the date of this annual report.
      計劃中可予發行的股份總數以及其於本年                               誠如綜合文件及聯合公告所披露，根據購股權計劃的條款，於二零二二年三
      報日期佔已發行股份的百分率：                                   月三日的所有未行使購股權已於二零二二年三月三日自動失效。因此，於本
                                                       年報日期並無未行使購股權。

      Maximum entitlement of each participant          Unless approved by the Shareholders, the total number of Shares issued and to be
      under the scheme:                                issued upon the exercise of the Share Options granted to each eligible person
                                                       (including exercised, cancelled and outstanding Share Options) in any 12-month
                                                       period shall not exceed 1% of the relevant class of securities of the Company in issue.
      計劃中每名參與者可獲授權益上限：                                 除非獲股東批准，否則於任何 12 個月期間內，因行使已授予各合資格人士的

The other information comprises all of the information included in the    年報內的所有信息，但不包括綜合財務報表及我們的
annual report other than the consolidated financial statements and our    核數師報告。
auditor’s report thereon.

the other information and we do not express any form of assurance         亦不對該等其他信息發表任何形式的鑒證結論。
conclusion thereon.

In connection with our audit of the consolidated financial statements,    結合我們對綜合財務報表的審計，我們的責任是閱讀

consider whether the other information is materially inconsistent with    務報表或我們在審計過程中所了解的情況存在重大抵
the consolidated financial statements or our knowledge obtained in        觸或者似乎存在重大錯誤陳述的情況。
the audit or otherwise appears to be materially misstated.

If, based on the work we have performed, we conclude that there is a      基於我們已執行的工作，如果我們認為其他信息存在
material misstatement of this other information, we are required to       重大錯誤陳述，我們需要報告該事實。在這方面，我
report that fact. We have nothing to report in this regard.               們沒有任何報告。

1.   GENERAL INFORMATION                                                    1.   一般資料
     i-CABLE Communications Limited (the “Company”) is a limited                 有線寬頻通訊有限公司（「本公司」）是一家於香港
     liability company incorporated in Hong Kong. The address of its             註冊成立的有限公司。其香港註冊辦事處地址為
     registered office in Hong Kong is 7th Floor, Cable TV Tower, 9 Hoi          香港荃灣海盛路九號有線電視大樓七樓。
     Shing Road, Tsuen Wan, Hong Kong.

     The Company has its primary listing on The Stock Exchange of                 本公司的股份主要在香港聯合交易所有限公司
     Hong Kong Limited (the “Stock Exchange”).                                   （「聯交所」）上市。

     The Company, its subsidiaries and consolidated structured                   本公司、其附屬公司及綜合結構性實體（統稱「本
     entities (together the “Group”) are engaged in television                   集團」）經營有關電視用戶服務的訂購、本地免費
     subscription business, domestic free television programme                   電 視 節 目 服 務、廣 告、頻 道 轉 播、電 視 轉 播 服
     services, advertising, channel carriage, television relay service,          務、節 目 特 許 權、戲 院 放 映、其 他 電 視 相 關 業
     programme licensing, theatrical release, other television related           務、寬頻上網服務、網站訂購、電話服務、網絡
     businesses, broadband internet access services, portal operation,           租賃、網絡建設、流動通訊服務及流動電話代理
     telephony services, network leasing, network construction,                  服務以及其他上網相關業務。
     mobile service and mobile agency service as well as other
     internet access related businesses.

     the board of directors (the “Directors”) of the Company on 31               由本公司董事（「董事」）會批准。
     March 2022.

2.   BASIS OF PREPARATION                                                   2.   編製基準
     The consolidated financial statements have been prepared in                 綜合財務報表乃按照香港會計師公會（「香港會計
     accordance with Hong Kong Financial Reporting Standards                     師公會」）頒佈的香港財務報告準則（「香港財務報
     (“HKFRS”) issued by the Hong Kong Institute of Certified Public             告準則」）而編製。除按公允價值計入損益（「按公
     Accountants (“HKICPA”). The consolidated financial statements               允價值計入損益」）的金融資產按公允價值計量
     have been prepared under the historical cost convention, except             外，該等綜合財務報表乃按歷史成本慣例編製。
     for financial assets at fair value through profit or loss (“FVTPL”),
     which are measured at fair value.

     The preparation of consolidated financial statements in                     編製符合香港財務報告準則的綜合財務報表須運
     conformity with HKFRS requires the use of certain critical                  用若干關鍵會計估計。管理層於應用本集團會計
     accounting estimates. It also requires management to exercise               政策時亦須作出判斷。涉及高度的判斷或高度複
     its judgement in the process of applying the Group’s accounting             雜性，或涉及對財務報表屬重大的假設及估算之
     policies. The areas involving a higher degree of judgement or               範疇於下文附註 4 披露。
     complexity, or areas where assumptions and estimates are
     significant to the consolidated financial statements are disclosed
     in Note 4 below.

      2.   BASIS OF PREPARATION (Continued)                                     2.   編製基準（續）
           During the year ended 31 December 2021, the Group incurred a              截至二零二一年十二月三十一日止年度，本集團
           net loss of HK$364 million (2020: HK$275 million) and as at 31            錄 得 淨 虧 損 364,000,000 港 元（ 二 零 二 零 年：
           December 2021, the Group’s current liabilities exceeded its               275,000,000 港元），而本集團於二零二一年十二月
           current assets by HK$410 million (2020: HK$413 million). Included         三十一日的流動負債較其流動資產超逾
           in its current liabilities was an interest-bearing borrowing of           410,000,000港元（二零二零年：413,000,000港元）。
           HK$295 million drawn from a banking facility of HK$400 million            其流動負債包括從銀行融資 400,000,000 港元中提
           which is immediately repayable on demand and subject to                   取的帶息貸款 295,000,000 港元，有關貸款須按要
           review at any time from the date of this report. Besides the              求立即償還，並須自本報告日期起隨時接受審

                       cost, adjusted for any excess of the Group’s share of                  投資公司可辨別資產淨值的公允價值
                       the acquisition date fair values of the investee’s                     超 過 該 投 資 成 本（如 適 用）而 作 出 調
                       identifiable net assets over the cost of the                           整。然後該投資就本集團所佔該被投
                       investment (if any). Thereafter, the investment is                     資公司資產淨值的收購後變動及與投
                       adjusted for the post acquisition change in the                        資有關的任何減值虧損作出調整（見
                       Group’s share of the investee’s net assets and any                     附註 3(p)(ii)）。綜合損益表反映在收購
                       impairment loss relating to the investment (see                        日的可辨別資產淨值的公允價值與本
                       Note 3(p)(ii)). Any acquisition-date excess over cost,                 集團投資成本的差額，年內本集團所
                       the Group’s share of the post-acquisition, post-tax                    佔被投資公司於收購後的除稅後業績
                       results of the investees and any impairment losses                     及任何減值虧損，綜合其他全面收益
                       for the year are recognised in the consolidated                        表反映本集團應佔該被投資公司於收
                       statement of profit or loss, whereas the Group’s                       購後之其他全面收益中的除稅後項目。
                       share of the post-acquisition, post-tax items of the

                       made payments on behalf of the investee. For this                      外。就此而言，本集團在聯營公司所

                       of the investment under the equity method                              面金額，以及實質上構成本集團在聯

     (c) Leases                                                                (c) 租賃
         Leases are recognised as a right-of-use asset and a                     租賃確認為使用權資產，並在租賃資產可
         corresponding liability at the date at which the leased                 供本集團使用之日確認相應負債。
         asset is available for use by the Group.

         Assets and liabilities arising from a lease are initially               租賃產生的資產及負債初始按現值基準計
         measured on a present value basis. Lease liabilities include            量。租賃負債包括固定付款（包括實質性的
         the net present value of the fixed payments (including in-              固定付款）的現值淨額，減任何應收租賃優
         substance fixed payments), less any lease incentives                    惠。根據合理確定續期選擇權作出的租賃
         receivable. Lease payments to be made under reasonably                  付款亦計入負債的計量中。
         certain extension options are also included in the
         measurement of the liability.

         The lease payments are discounted using the interest rate               租賃付款採用租賃所隱含的利率予以貼現。
         implicit in the lease. If that rate cannot be readily                   倘無法釐定該利率，則一般就本集團租賃
         determined, which is generally the case for leases in the               而言，會使用承租人的增量借款利率，即
         Group, the lessee’s incremental borrowing rate is used,                 個別承租人在類似條款、抵押及條件的類
         being the rate that the individual lessee would have to                 似經濟環境中借入獲得類似使用權資產價
         pay to borrow the funds necessary to obtain an asset of                 值資產所需資金所必須支付的利率。本集
         similar value to the right-of-use asset in a similar economic           團使用最近收到就租賃條款作出的特定調
         environment with similar terms, security and conditions.                整的第三方融資釐定增量借款利率。
         The Group determines the incremental borrowing rate by
         using recent third-party financing received with
         adjustments specific to the term of the leases.

         Lease payments are allocated between principal and                      租賃付款在本金和融資費用之間分配。融
         finance cost. The finance cost is charged to profit or loss             資費用在租賃期內從損益中扣除，以就每
         over the lease period so as to produce a constant periodic              個期間的負債餘額產生固定的定期利率。
         rate of interest on the remaining balance of the liability for
         each period.

                        Computer software and website development costs                          不符合上述標準的電腦軟件及網站開
                        that do not meet the above criteria are expensed in                      發費用於產生時在綜合損益表支銷。
                        the consolidated statement of profit or loss as
                        incurred.

           (f)   Inventories                                                        (f)   存貨
                 Inventories are carried at the lower of cost and net                     存貨以成本與可變現淨值兩者中較低者列
                 realisable value. Cost is calculated on the weighted                     賬。成本乃按加權平均基準計算，並包括
                 average basis and comprises all costs of purchase, costs of              所有採購成本、加工成本及令存貨達致現
                 conversion and other costs incurred in bringing the                      狀之其他成本。可變現淨值為日常業務中
                 inventories to their present location and condition. Net                 的估計售價減去估計完工成本及進行銷售
                 realisable value is the estimated selling price in the                   所需的估計成本。
                 ordinary course of business less the estimated costs of
                 completion and the estimated costs necessary to make
                 the sale.

     (i) Revenue recognition (Continued)                                      (i) 收入之確認（續）
         Incremental costs incurred to obtain a contract with a                 倘本集團預期收回該等成本，則取得與客
         customer are capitalised as contract acquisition costs if the          戶的合約所產生的增量成本資本化為合約
         Group expects to recover these costs. Costs of obtaining a             收購成本。獲得合約的成本按特定合約的
         contract are amortised on a straight-line basis over the               期限以直線法攤銷。作為實際權宜之計，
         terms of the specific contracts. As a practical expedient,             倘本集團原應確認的資產攤銷期間為 1 年或
         the Group recognises the incremental cost of obtaining a               更短，則本集團於產生時將取得合約的增
         contract as an expense when incurred if the amortisation               加成本確認為開支。
         period of the asset that the Group otherwise would have
         recognised is 1 year or less.

         The period between the transfer of promised goods and                  向客戶轉讓承諾商品及服務以及客戶付款
         services to the customers and payments by customers                    之間的期限通常在 1 年之內，因此，沒有融
         usually is within 1 year, as a result, there is no financing           資部分需要調整交易價格以獲得貨幣的時
         component which requires adjustment of the transaction                 間價值。
         prices for the time value of money.

         If the payments by customers exceed the services                       倘客戶付款超過所提供服務，則合約負債
         rendered, a contract liability is recognised as receipts in            會於綜合財務狀況表中確認為預收賬款。
         advance on the consolidated statement of financial                     倘若所提供的服務超過客戶的付款及到目
         position. If the services rendered exceed the payments by              前為止對合約代價的無條件權利，則合約
         customers and unconditional rights to contract                         資產會在綜合財務狀況表中確認。
         consideration to date, a contract asset is recognised on
         the consolidated statement of financial position.

                     estimated future cash flows are discounted to                        的 計 算 方 法，是 估 計 將 來 的 現
                     their present value using a pre-tax discount                         金 流 量，以 稅 前 之 貼 現 率 計 至
                     rate that reflects current market assessments                        現 值。貼 現 率 應 能 反 映 當 前 由
                     of the time value of money and the risks                             市場評估的金錢時間值及該項

                     independently (i.e. a cash-generating unit).

     (r) Financial guarantees issued, provisions                               (r) 所發出之財務擔保、撥備及或然

         (i)   Financial guarantees issued                                       (i)   所發出之財務擔保
               Financial guarantees are contracts that require the                     財務擔保乃要求發行人（即擔保人）就
               issuer (i.e. the guarantor) to make specified                           擔保受益（「持有人」）因特定債務人未
               payments to reimburse the beneficiary of the                            能根據債項工具的條款於到期時付款
               guarantee (the “holder”) for a loss the holder incurs                   而蒙受的損失，而向持有人支付特定
               because a specified debtor fails to make payment                        款項的合約。
               when due in accordance with the terms of a debt
               instrument.

               Financial guarantee contracts are recognised as a                       在擔保發出的同時，財務擔保合約確
               financial liability at the time the guarantee is issued.                認為金融負債。該負債初始按公允價
               The liability is initially measured at fair value and                   值計量並且其後按以下兩者之更高者
               subsequently at the higher of                                           計量：

               —     the amount determined in accordance with                          —   根據《香港財務報告準則》第 9 號
                     the expected credit loss model under HKFRS 9                          「金融工具」項下之預期信用損
                     “Financial Instruments”; and                                          失模式釐定的金額；及

               —     the amount initially recognised less, where                       —   初始確認的金額減去，如適用，
                     appropriate, the cumulative amount of                                 根據《香港財務報告準則》第 15
                     income recognised in accordance with the                              號「客戶合約收入」準則確認的
                     principles of HKFRS 15 “Revenue from                                  累計收入金額。
                     Contracts with Customers”.

               The fair value of financial guarantees is determined                    財務擔保的公允價值乃根據該債務工
               based on the present value of the difference in cash                    具下規定的合約付款與無擔保情況下
               flows between the contractual payments required                         所需的付款之間的現金流量差額之現
               under the debt instrument and the payments that                         值或為承擔責任而應付第三方之估計
               would be required without the guarantee, or the                         金額而釐定。
               estimated amount that would be payable to a third
               party for assuming the obligations.

                of deferred tax assets at the end of each reporting period,              資產之賬面值。預測會因應新業務發展及
                based on the forecast results of the Group and the                       已批准業務計劃計入預期業務增長。在錄
                forecasts of future taxable profits of the relevant entities             得近期虧損的情況下評估是否有可靠憑證

                relate. The currency giving rise to this risk is primarily

          different valuation methods. The inputs to valuation                        值方法計量。估值方法的輸入數據在公允
          methods are categorised into three levels within a fair                     價值層級中分為以下三個級別：
          value hierarchy, as follows:

          Level 1:   The fair value of financial instruments traded                   第一級： 在活躍市場中交易的金融工具
                     in active markets (such as publicly traded                           （例如公開買賣的衍生工具及股
                     derivatives, and equity securities) is based on                       票證券）的公允價值乃基於報告
                     quoted market prices at the end of the                                期 結 算 日 的 市 場 報 價。本 集 團
                     reporting period. The quoted market price                             持有的金融資產使用的市場報
                     used for financial assets held by the Group is                        價 為 當 前 買 入 價。則 該 工 具 計
                     the current bid price. These instruments are                          入第一級。
                     included in Level 1.

          Level 2:   The fair value of financial instruments that are                 第二級： 並非在活躍市場中交易的金融
                     not traded in an active market (for example,                          工具（例如場外衍生工具）的公
                     over-the-counter derivatives) is determined                           允 價 值 採 用 估 值 技 術 釐 定，該
                     using valuation techniques which maximise                             估值技術會盡量利用可觀察市
                     the use of observable market data and rely as                         場 數 據，並 盡 可 能 減 少 依 賴 實
                     little as possible on entity-specific estimates. If                   體 個 別 的 估 算。倘 若 計 算 公 允
                     all significant inputs required to fair value an                      價值所需的所有重大輸入資料
                     instrument are observable, the instrument is                          均 可 觀 察，則 該 工 具 計 入 第 二
                     included in Level 2.                                                  級。

          Level 3:   If one or more of the significant inputs is not                  第三級： 倘若一項或多項重要輸入數據
                     based on observable market data, the                                  並 非 基 於 可 觀 察 的 市 場 數 據，
                     instrument is included in Level 3.                                    則該工具計入第三級。

      6.   REVENUE                                                               6.   收入
           The principal activity of the Company is investment holding. The           本公司之主要業務是投資控股。本公司主要附屬
           principal activities of the principal subsidiaries and consolidated        公司及綜合結構性實體之主要業務載列於綜合財
           structured entities of the Company set out in Note 18 to the               務報表附註 18。
           consolidated financial statements.

           Revenue comprises principally subscription, service and related            收入主要包括電視、寬頻上網服務及電話用戶服
